#Lorent ideas 3
A01_ideas_3 = {
	start = { #LENCORI TRADITIONS
		cavalry_cost = -0.20 # -0.10/-0.15/-0.20
		diplomatic_reputation = 2 #1/1.5/2
	}
	bonus = { #LORENTISH AMBITION
		heavy_ship_power = 0.10
        light_ship_power = 0.10
        galley_power = 0.10
        transport_power = 0.10
	}

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = CoT_ideas_lorent
		has_country_flag = CoT_ideas_tier_3
	}
	free = yes		#will be added at load.

	A01_idea_1_3 = { #Adeanite Fervour, LORENTISH UNIQUE IDEA 1
		cavalry_power = 0.20
        cav_to_inf_ratio = 0.50
	}
	A01_idea_2_3 = { #VINES AND VINEYARDS, LENCORI CULTURAL IDEA 2
		global_unrest = -2 #-1/-1.5/-2
        global_trade_goods_size_modifier = 0.10 #0.05/0.075/0.10
	}
	A01_idea_3_3 = { #Love thy ELVEN neighbour, LORENTISH UNIQUE IDEA 3
		monarch_lifespan = 5
	}
	A01_idea_4_3 = { #Hereditary Hierarchy, LENCORI CULTURAL IDEA 4
		liberty_desire_from_subject_development = -0.33 #-0.15/-0.25/-0.33
	}
	A01_idea_5_3 = { #Halfings, Elves, Dwarves, LORENTISH UNIQUE IDEA 5
		global_manpower_modifier = 0.10
        discipline = 0.025
        siege_ability = 0.10
	}
	A01_idea_6_3 = { #Noble Officers, LENCORI CULTURAL IDEA 6
		army_tradition_decay = -0.01 #-0.005 / -0.0075 / -0.01
        free_leader_pool = 3 #1/2/3
	}
	A01_idea_7_3 = { #Rose Resplendent! LORENTISH UNIQUE IDEA 7
		legitimacy = 1.5
        devotion = 1.5
        republican_tradition = 0.5
	}
}
